data-postid="post-121232" id="content" role="main"><section class="container row hero-row hero-short default-bg row-shadow full-scr"><div class="anim-wrapper secondary-hero"> <span class="fade-in-left anim-fill"><img src="/wp-content/themes/Aruba2015/images/slices/anim-a-fill-orange.svg"/></span> <span class="fade-in-left anim-dots"><noscript><img src="/wp-content/themes/Aruba2015/images/slices/anim-b-dotted-white.png"/></noscript><img class="lazyload" data-src="/wp-content/themes/Aruba2015/images/slices/anim-b-dotted-white.png" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20210%20140%22%3E%3C/svg%3E"/></span> <span class="fade-in-left anim-lines"><noscript><img src="/wp-content/themes/Aruba2015/images/slices/anim-u-outline-white_secondary-hero.svg"/></noscript><img class="lazyload" data-src="/wp-content/themes/Aruba2015/images/slices/anim-u-outline-white_secondary-hero.svg" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20210%20140%22%3E%3C/svg%3E"/></span></div><div class="lazyload hero-bg" data-bg="https://www.arubanetworks.com/wp-content/uploads/header-gen-1-short-hero_795x253.jpg" style="background-image: url(data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20300%22%3E%3C/svg%3E)"><div class="col-wrap"><div class="hero-wrapper colspan-7"><div class="txt-wrapper"><ul class="breadcrumbs" data-swiftype-index="false"><li><a href="https://www.arubanetworks.com">Home</a></li><li class="separator"> /</li><li class="endBread"> Data Privacy</li></ul><h1>Data Privacy</h1></div></div></div></div></section><section class="container row overview-row bg-none"><div class="col-wrap"><div class="colspan-12 flex-cols flex-middle img-right"><div class="colspan-6 block-text"><h2>Overview</h2><div class="overview-intro intro">Aruba, a Hewlett Packard Enterprise company, respects the privacy of our customers, employees, partners, and other stakeholders.  Ensuring privacy is not just a core value at Aruba, it is integral to the way we do business and the way we build our products and services.  We are committed to accountability and seek to maintain a robust privacy program consistent with our <a href="https://www.hpe.com/us/en/legal/privacy.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">global privacy policy</a>.</div></div><div class="colspan-5 block-img"> <noscript><img class="attachment-full right-left" src="https://www.arubanetworks.com/wp-content/uploads/overview-module_indoor-ap-b_640x605.png"/></noscript><img class="lazyload attachment-full right-left" data-src="https://www.arubanetworks.com/wp-content/uploads/overview-module_indoor-ap-b_640x605.png" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20210%20140%22%3E%3C/svg%3E"/></div></div></div></section><section class="container row content-block block-columns-row"><div class="anim-wrapper product-subcat-contentC"> <span class="fade-in-left anim-stripes go"><noscript><img src="/wp-content/themes/Aruba2015/images/slices/anim-a-stripes-blood-orange-reverse.png"/></noscript><img class="lazyload" data-src="/wp-content/themes/Aruba2015/images/slices/anim-a-stripes-blood-orange-reverse.png" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20210%20140%22%3E%3C/svg%3E"/></span><br/> <span class="fade-in-left anim-lines go"><noscript><img src="/wp-content/themes/Aruba2015/images/slices/anim-c-outline-skyblue.svg"/></noscript><img class="lazyload" data-src="/wp-content/themes/Aruba2015/images/slices/anim-c-outline-skyblue.svg" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20210%20140%22%3E%3C/svg%3E"/></span></div><div class="col-wrap left-aligned"><div class="glossary-text left-aligned center columns-2"><h2>Aruba Product and Service Privacy</h2><p></p><ul><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/Aruba_Products_GDPR_DataPrivacySecurityAgreement.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Data Privacy and Security Agreement for all Aruba Products &amp; Services</a></li></ul><div class="no-column-break"><h2>Aruba Product Specific Privacy and Security Data Sheets</h2><p></p><p>In addition to the general DPSA, Aruba provides detailed privacy and security data sheets for several individual products.  Each data sheet is referenced in the Data Privacy and Security Agreement for Aruba Products &amp; Services. The data sheets identify the: (i) products functionalities and performance, (ii) customer personal data processed, (iii) data subjects to whom the personal data pertain, (iv) scope of the processing activities, (v) security and encryption features, and (vi) certifications.</p><p>Product-specific data sheets:</p><ul><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_AirWave.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba AirWave</a></li><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_ArubaOS.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba ArubaOS</a></li><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_Central.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba Central</a></li><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_ClearPass.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba ClearPass</a></li><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_ClearPass-Device-Insight.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba ClearPass Device Insight</a></li><li><a href="https://www.arubainstanton.com/dpsa/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba Instant On</a></li><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_Introspect.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba IntroSpect</a></li><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_Meridian.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba Meridian</a></li><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_NetInsight.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba NetInsight</a></li><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_Workplace-Insights.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Aruba Workplace Insights</a></li><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/GDPR_Supplement_User-Experience-Insight.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">User Experience Insight</a></li></ul></div><h2>GDPR Compliance</h2><p></p><p>The General Data Protection Regulation (“GDPR”) is a landmark piece of European data protection legislation which strengthens and unifies data protection for individuals within the European Union (EU). It impacts every organization that processes European personal data both inside and outside Europe and introduced increased compliance requirements and significant financial penalties for companies that fail to comply. The GDPR was passed in May 2016 and came into force in May 2018.  Not only is Aruba GDPR compliant, but Aruba’s products and services can help our customer’s maintain GDPR compliance.</p><p>Learn more:</p><ul><li><a href="/assets/gdpr/Aruba_GDPR_CustomerCommunication.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Customer Communication</a></li><li><a href="/assets/wp/WP_SecuritySolutionsGDPR.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">"Aruba Security Solutions for GDPR" White Paper </a></li></ul></div></div></section></div></div><div class="footer" data-swiftype-index="false"><div class="inner"><div
